&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;−&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The &quot;Willow Song&quot; which follows is marked by an increasing orchestral sound, with woodwinds and strings adding to it, yet what compounds the sadness of the piece is the wail-like cries of &quot;Salce&quot; made by Desdemona followed by similarly despairing, yet softer &quot;echoes&quot; played by the English horn. Near the end of the song, Desdemona's fear, which has been hidden up to this point by a veil of sadness, is made apparent; she mistakes the noise of the wind for that of an intruder. The orchestra immediately builds to a fortissimo, reflecting the genuine worries possessed by Desdemona. The music that gradually lessens with the comforting of Emilia and returns for a final repetition of the theme of the &quot;Willow Song&quot;.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The &quot;Willow Song&quot; which follows is marked by an increasing orchestral sound, with woodwinds and strings adding to it, yet what compounds the sadness of the piece is the wail-like cries of &quot;&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;''&lt;/ins&gt;Salce&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;''&lt;/ins&gt;&quot; made by Desdemona followed by similarly despairing, yet softer &quot;echoes&quot; played by the English horn. Near the end of the song, Desdemona's fear, which has been hidden up to this point by a veil of sadness, is made apparent; she mistakes the noise of the wind for that of an intruder. The orchestra immediately builds to a fortissimo, reflecting the genuine worries possessed by Desdemona. The music that gradually lessens with the comforting of Emilia and returns for a final repetition of the theme of the &quot;Willow Song&quot;.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: sol
1000
id; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Afterwards, Desdemona begins to bid Emilia adieu. This goodbye is initially accompanied by repeated notes on the lower woodwinds and strings such as those in the introduction of the act but in a much more noticeable and dominating manner. This reflects the increasing expectation of Desdemona of her death. Initially, she attempts to keep these feelings to herself, but the orchestra reveals her increasing inner thoughts. These feelings finally reach a point at which they can no longer be contained and Desdemona lets out a loud passionate cry of goodbye to Emilia, one that is reinforced by the full orchestral accompaniment.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Afterwards, Desdemona begins to bid Emilia adieu. This goodbye is initially accompanied by repeated notes on the lower woodwinds and strings such as those in the introduction of the act but in a much more noticeable and dominating manner. This reflects the increasing expectation of Desdemona of her death. Initially, she attempts to keep these feelings to herself, but the orchestra reveals her increasing inner thoughts. These feelings finally reach a point at which they can no longer be contained and Desdemona lets out a loud passionate cry of goodbye to Emilia, one that is reinforced by the full orchestral accompaniment.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;

With a population of approximately &lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;12&lt;/del&gt;,000+&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;http://&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;wikimapia&lt;/del&gt;.&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;org&lt;/del&gt;/&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;6186579&lt;/del&gt;/&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;La-Horquetta&lt;/del&gt;&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;, it is located in the South Eastern corner of the Tunapuna-Piarco Region, La Horquetta is bounded by the [[Churchill Roosevelt Highway]] to the north, Arima river to the west Brazil river to the south and the [[Aripo Savannas]] to the east and is adjacent to two other Arima neighborhoods: [[Malabar, Trinidad and Tobago|Malabar]] to the north, and Carapo to the east. La Horquetta is patrolled by the [[Trinidad and Tobago Police Service]]'s, La Horquetta Department, Aswell as Neighborhood Watch and the national organization, Community Comfort Patrol. La Horquetta is dividing into 8 sections, Phase 1, Phase 2, Phase 3, Phase 4, Phase 5, Phase 6, Phase 7 and the newly built Greenvale Park. It also claims the title of being one of the largest housing project completed by the Government of [[Trinidad and Tobago]].&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;==United States==&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;−&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;In the United States, associate &lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;degrees&lt;/del&gt; are usually earned in two years or less and can be attained at [[community colleges]], [[technical college]]s, [[vocational schools]], and some [[colleges]]. A student who completes a two-year program can earn an '''Associate of Arts''' (A.A.) or an '''Associate of Science''' (A.S.). A.A. degrees are usually earned in humanities, business, and social science fields. A.S. degrees are awarded to those studying in scientific and technical fields. Students who complete a two-year technical or vocational program can earn an '''Associate of Applied Science''' (A.A.S., easily confused with the Associate of Arts and Science). Th
1000
ey may also have the option to use the credits from the associate degree toward a bachelor's degree.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web|url=http://www.collegezone.com/415_813.htm |title=Student Zone – College – Finding/Applying |publisher=College Zone |date= |accessdate=2013-07-25}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;In the United States, associate &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;daprees&lt;/ins&gt; are usually earned in two years or less and can be attained at [[community colleges]], [[technical college]]s, [[vocational schools]], and some [[colleges]]. A student who completes a two-year program can earn an '''Associate of Arts''' (A.A.) or an '''Associate of Science''' (A.S.). A.A. degrees are usually earned in humanities, business, and social science fields. A.S. degrees are awarded to those studying in scientific and technical fields. Students who complete a two-year technical or vocational program can earn an '''Associate of Applied Science''' (A.A.S., easily confused with the Associate of Arts and Science). They may also have the option to use the credits from the associate degree toward a bachelor's degree.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web|url=http://www.collegezone.com/415_813.htm |title=Student Zone – College – Finding/Applying |publisher=College Zone |date= |accessdate=2013-07-25}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;::::::If it cheers you up, I agree that it is true that, given just the problem stated by you, using my knowledege of probability, game shows, and life in general that I would probably switch.  We know that there are circumstances where there is a clear advantage to switching (for example MHP with standard assumptions) and there are not many realistic scenarios where it would be a disadvantage to switch, so overall, switching is probably the best strategy.  If that is your point then fine, it is a valid observation.  However, it has as more to do with real world experience than it does with probability it it is not the reason that the MHP is so infamous.  The MHP, when understood as most people naturally do, is a simple brain teaser that most people get wrong, not an exercise in intuitive Bayesian estimation. [[User:Martin Hogbin|Martin Hogbin]] ([[User talk:Martin Hogbin|talk]]) 15:48, 17 October 2015 (UTC)&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The standard assumptions are those that most people make when they answer the question.  They are based on people's knowledge of game shows in general and what people thought that vos Savant's precise question was intended to be.  They cannot be challenged using mathematics or logic.  First you decide, on whatever basis you choose, what the exact question is, then mathematics gives you the unequivocal answer. They are based on people's knowledge of game shows in general and what people thought that vos Savant's precise question was intended to be.  They cannot be challenged using mathematics or logic.  First you decide, on whatever basis you choose, what the exact question is, then mathematics gives you the unequivocal answer. He also wrote art songs for solo voice with piano accompaniment, including ‘''Mynuly lita molodii''’ (The Years of Youth Have Passed By); arrangements of folk songs for solo voice or choir; and Vitrohony, a cycle of kolomyika melodies for piano.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

1000
1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The &lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;[[BWF Super Series|&lt;/del&gt;BWF Superseries&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;]]&lt;/del&gt;, launched on&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; 14&lt;/del&gt; December 2006 and implemented in 2007,&amp;lt;ref name=1a&amp;gt;{{cite news|title=BWF Launches Super Series|url=http://www.badminton.org.au/index.php?id=22&amp;amp;tx_ttnews%5Btt_news%5D=136&amp;amp;tx_ttnews%5BbackPid%5D=2&amp;amp;cHash=26fb36d8a5|newspaper=Badminton Australia|date=&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;15 December &lt;/del&gt;2006}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; is a series of elite badminton tournaments, sanctioned by [[Badminton World Federation]] (BWF). A season of Superseries features twelve tournaments around the world&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;, including five elevated as Premier Series&lt;/del&gt;, which introduced since 2011,&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite news|title=Yonex All England Elevated To BWF Premier Super Series Event|url=http://www.ibadmintonstore.com/iBADMINTONstore-News/Yonex-All-England-Elevated-To-BWF-Premier-Super-Se.aspx|accessdate=29 September 2013|newspaper=Badmintonstore.com}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; with successful players invited to the Superseries&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; Masters&lt;/del&gt; Finals held at the year end.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;'''&lt;/ins&gt;BWF Superseries&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;'''&lt;/ins&gt;, launched on December&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; 14,&lt;/ins&gt; 2006 and implemented in &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;[[&lt;/ins&gt;2007&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; in badminton|2007]]&lt;/ins&gt;,&amp;lt;ref name=1a&amp;gt;{{cite news|title=BWF Launches Super Series|url=http://www.badminton.org.au/index.php?id=22&amp;amp;tx_ttnews%5Btt_news%5D=136&amp;amp;tx_ttnews%5BbackPid%5D=2&amp;amp;cHash=26fb36d8a5|newspaper=Badminton Australia|date=2006&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;-12-15&lt;/ins&gt;}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; is a series of elite badminton tournaments, sanctioned by [[Badminton World Federation]] (BWF)&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;. BWF Superseries has two level such as [[BWF Superseries|Superseries and Superseries Premier]]&lt;/ins&gt;. A season of Superseries features twelve tournaments around the world, which introduced since 2011,&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite news|title=Yonex All England Elevated To BWF Premier Super Series Event|url=http://www.ibadmintonstore.com/iBADMINTONstore-News/Yonex-All-England-Elevated-To-BWF-Premier-Super-Se.aspx|accessdate=29 September 2013|newspaper=Badmintonstore.com}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; with successful players invited to the&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; [[BWF&lt;/ins&gt; Superseries Finals&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;]]&lt;/ins&gt; held at the year end.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

ffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;to&lt;/del&gt; the [[Caribbean]] island of [[Barbados]].&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The '''Barbados threadsnake''' ('''''Leptotyphlops carlae''''') is a [[species]] of blind [[Leptotyphlopidae|threadsnake]]. It is the smallest&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; known&lt;/ins&gt; [[snake]] species.&amp;lt;ref name=&quot;zootaxa&quot;/&amp;gt; This member of the [[Leptotyphlopidae]] [[Family (biology)|family]] is &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;found only&lt;/ins&gt; &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;on&lt;/ins&gt; the [[Caribbean]] island of [[Barbados]].&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;

  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

Blair Hedges]], a [[&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;Biology&lt;/del&gt;|&lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;biologist&lt;/del&gt;]] from [[Pennsylvania State University]].&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite news|url=http://uk.reuters.com/article/UKNews1/idUKN0151253520080803|title=World's smallest snake is as thin as spaghetti|author=Dunham, Will|date=August 3, 2008|accessdate=2008-08-04|publisher=Reuters UK| archiveurl= http://web.archive.org/web/20080902051450/http://uk.reuters.com/article/UKNews1/idUKN0151253520080803| archivedate= 2 September 2008 &amp;lt;!--DASHBot--&amp;gt;| deadurl= no}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; Hedges named the new species of snake in honor of his wife, Carla Ann Hass, a [[herpetology|herpetologist]] who was part of the discovery team.&amp;lt;ref name=&quot;eflux&quot;&amp;gt;{{cite news|url=http://www.efluxmedia.com/news_Worlds_Smallest_Snake_Discovered_on_the_Caribbean_Island_of_Barbados_21414.html|title=World's Smallest Snake Discovered on the Caribbean Island of Barbados|author=Turner, Alice|date=August 3, 2008|accessdate=2008-08-04|publisher=eFluxMedia| archiveurl= http://web.archive.org/web/20080806185328/http://www.efluxmedia.com/news_Worlds_Smallest_Snake_Discovered_on_the_Caribbean_Island_of_Barbados_21414.html| archivedate= 6 August 2008 &amp;lt;!--DASHBot--&amp;gt;| deadurl= no}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;Beolens, Bo; Watkins, Michael; Grayson, Michael (2011). ''The Eponym Dictionary of Reptiles''. Baltimore: Johns Hopkins University Press. xiii + 296 pp. ISBN 978-1-4214-0135-5. (''Leptotyphlops carlae'', p. 48).&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; Specimens already existed in reference collections in the London [[Natural History Museum, London|Natural History Museum]] and in a museum in California, but they had been incorrectly identified to belong to another species.&amp;lt;ref name=&quot;zootaxa&quot;/&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

''The Eponym Dictionary of Reptiles''. Baltimore: Johns Hopkins University Press. xiii + 296 pp. ISBN 978-1-4214-0135-5. (''Leptotyphlops carlae'', p. 48).&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; Specimens already existed in reference collections in the London [[Natural History Museum, London|Natural History Museum]] and in a museum in California, but they had been incorrectly identified to belong to another species.&amp;lt;ref name=&quot;zootaxa&quot;/&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

1000
chive.org/web/20080905235530/http://www.eurekalert.org/pub_releases/2008-08/ps-wss072808.php| archivedate= 5 September 2008 &amp;lt;!--DASHBot--&amp;gt;| deadurl= no}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; The first scientific specimens taken by the research team were found under rocks in a forest. The snake is thought to be near the lower size limit for snakes, as young snakes need to attain a certain minimum size to find suitable food.&amp;lt;ref name=&quot;eureka&quot;/&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

	<entry>
		<id>https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Key_(lock)&amp;diff=686187267&amp;oldid=686187001</id>
		<title>Key (lock)</title>
		<link rel="alternate" type="text/html" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Key_(lock)&amp;diff=686187267&amp;oldid=686187001"/>
				<updated>2015-10-17T15:48:24Z</updated>
		
		<summary type="html">&lt;p&gt;‎&lt;span dir=&quot;auto&quot;&gt;&lt;span class=&quot;autocomment&quot;&gt;Tubular key&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
&lt;table class='diff diff-contentalign-left'&gt;
				&lt;col class='diff-marker' /&gt;
				&lt;col class='diff-content' /&gt;
				&lt;col class='diff-marker' /&gt;
				&lt;col class='diff-content' /&gt;
				&lt;tr style='vertical-align: top;' lang='en'&gt;
				&lt;td colspan='2' style=&quot;background-color: white; color:black; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;← Previous revision&lt;/td&gt;
				&lt;td colspan='2' style=&quot;background-color: white; color:black; text-align: center;&quot;&gt;Revision as of 15:48, 17 October 2015&lt;/td&gt;
				&lt;/tr&gt;&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td colspan=&quot;2&quot; class=&quot;diff-lineno&quot;&gt;Line 137:&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td colspan=&quot;2&quot; class=&quot;diff-lineno&quot;&gt;Line 137:&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;A tubular key (sometimes referred to as a barrel key when describing a vintage or antique model) is one that is designed to open a [[tubular pin tumbler lock]]. It has a hollow, cylindrical shaft that is usually much shorter and has a larger diameter than most conventional keys. Antique or vintage-style barrel keys often closely resemble the more traditional skeleton key but are a more recent innovation in keymaking. In modern keys of this type, a number of grooves of varying length are built into the outer surface at the end of the shaft. These grooves are parallel to the shaft and allow the pins in the lock to slide to the end of the groove. A small tab on the outer surface of the shaft prevents the pins in the lock from pushing the key out and works with the hollow center to guide the key as it is turned.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;A tubular key (sometimes referred to as a barrel key when describing a vintage or antique model) is one that is designed to open a [[t
1000
ubular pin tumbler lock]]. It has a hollow, cylindrical shaft that is usually much shorter and has a larger diameter than most conventional keys. Antique or vintage-style barrel keys often closely resemble the more traditional skeleton key but are a more recent innovation in keymaking. In modern keys of this type, a number of grooves of varying length are built into the outer surface at the end of the shaft. These grooves are parallel to the shaft and allow the pins in the lock to slide to the end of the groove. A small tab on the outer surface of the shaft prevents the pins in the lock from pushing the key out and works with the hollow center to guide the key as it is turned.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;−&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The modern version of this type of key is harder to duplicate as it is less common and requires a different machine from regular keys. These keys are most often seen in home alarm systems, [[vending machine]]s, [[laptop lock]]s, and [[bicycle lock]]s, in the United States. These keys typically come in seven and eight-pin versions as well as miniature versions used on computers. Tubular keys were invented by the Chicago Lock company in Chicago, IL under the ACE Branding.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web|url=http://files.grimmelmann.net/cases/ChicagoLock.pdf|title=Chicago Lock Co., v. Morris V. Fanberg and Victor Fanberg|accessdate=22 May 2015}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The modern version of this type of key is harder to duplicate as it is less common and requires a different machine from regular keys. These keys are most often seen in home alarm systems, [[vending machine]]s, [[laptop lock]]s, and [[bicycle lock]]s, in the United States. These keys typically come in seven and eight-pin versions as well as miniature versions used on computers. Tubular keys were invented&lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt; in 1934&lt;/ins&gt; by the Chicago Lock company in Chicago, IL under the ACE Branding.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web|url=http://files.grimmelmann.net/cases/ChicagoLock.pdf|title=Chicago Lock Co., v. Morris V. Fanberg and Victor Fanberg|accessdate=22 May 2015}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;

P&amp;amp;S was a student group dedicated to bringing humor to student government via absurdist and playful pranks. In 1978 [[Leon Varjian]] ran for Student Senate and [[Jim Mallon]] ran for president of the Student Senate, both under the Pail &amp;amp; Shovel banner.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

1000
ent Senate race in the 1970s. P&amp;amp;S was a student group dedicated to bringing humor to student government via absurdist and playful pranks. In 1978 [[Leon Varjian]] ran for Student Senate and [[Jim Mallon]] ran for president of the Student Senate, both under the Pail &amp;amp; Shovel banner.&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

They aided the troupe members [[Gamora|Madam Gomorrah]], [[Star-Lord|Peadar O'Cuill]], [[Drax the Destroyer|Arthur Dubhghlas]], [[Groot|Goodman Root]], and [[Rocket Raccoon|Aroughcun the Raccoon]] to kill the beasts. As the creatures had traces of Enchantress' magic on them indicating she was somewhere nearby, Angela and Serah traveled with the Gardiner's Men to a pagan village in the outskirts of [[York]] where a marriage for the town beauty [[She-Venom|Anne Weying]] and the young [[Printer (publishing)|printer]]'s apprentice [[Eddie Brock|Edwin Brocc]] was going to happen. As the festival proceeded, Angela realized young Edwin had enchanted his bride to marry him when she saw him giving her a potion to drink. Edwin noticed Angela was seeing and panicked becoming a venomous monster and attacking her. Angela and her companions engaged him in battle and subdued him, afterwards Angela decapitated him. While leaving the town, Serah told Angela she wasn't afraid of her fate as long as Angela was with her.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;''1602: Witch Hunter Angela'' #2&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;

  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Angela and Serah then headed to Castle Caldecote, in Cumberland, as it was the whereabouts of the third Faustian. Her name was Anna Maria, the natural daughter of a bishop that was kept safe by Master Coulson in one of the castle's room, as instructed by her father. However, in the last new moon, she managed to escape the castle and returned somewhat different. Seeing the girl was not mad as Coulson said she was, Serah demanded the girl to be freed from her chains and told Angela to keep an eye on her. As the days passed, Serah, who had been studying about the Faerie, discovered that the Enchantress sends a sliver of herself into each of those with who she strike a deal and that she was using stories, such as that of her victims and Marlowe's play, to expand her power. Upon figuring it out, Serah started to devise a plan to counter that of Enchantress. Meanwhile, Angela struck a deal with Anna Maria: in exchange for a way to free her, she would tell Angela the truth about herself. The girl then told her she was born Witchbreed and that she eventually learned her touch was death. When the path to the Faerie was open, she took the opportunity to become something other than what she was, willingly strucking a deal with the Enchantress and becoming a Faustian. Later that night, Angela heard strange noises coming from Anna Maria's room and went to check if everything was right. There she found the girl cryi
1000
ng, frightened by the Enchantress' voice inside her head. The girl asked Angela to tell her a story to calm her down, and so she did, but was in vain as the Enchantress took control of the girl's body and attacked Angela. The girl managed to regain consciousness though and in an attempt to be free again, used Angela's weapon to kill herself. Serah showed up and was able to revive the girl, who was a Faustian no more. As she hasn't died, Serah tought she was safe from the Enchantress' wrath, but she was wrong as the Faerie rose from the blood of her lost Faustian and took Serah's life, fulfilling her menace. &lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Angela and Serah then headed to Castle Caldecote, in Cumberland, as it was the whereabouts of the third Faustian. Her name was Anna Maria, the natural daughter of a bishop that was kept safe by Master Coulson in one of the castle's room, as instructed by her father. However, in the last new moon, she managed to escape the castle and returned somewhat different. Seeing the girl was not mad as Coulson said she was, Serah demanded the girl to be freed from her chains and told Angela to keep an eye on her. As the days passed, Serah, who had been studying about the Faerie, discovered that the Enchantress sends a sliver of herself into each of those with who she strike a deal and that she was using stories, such as that of her victims and Marlowe's play, to expand her power. Upon figuring it out, Serah started to devise a plan to counter that of Enchantress. Meanwhile, Angela struck a deal with Anna Maria: in exchange for a way to free her, she would tell Angela the truth about herself. The girl then told her she was born Witchbreed and that she eventually learned her touch was death. When the path to the Faerie was open, she took the opportunity to become something other than what she was, willingly strucking a deal with the Enchantress and becoming a Faustian. Later that night, Angela heard strange noises coming from Anna Maria's room and went to check if everything was right. There she found the girl crying, frightened by the Enchantress' voice inside her head. The girl asked Angela to tell her a story to calm her down, and so she did, but was in vain as the Enchantress took control of the girl's body and attacked Angela. The girl managed to regain consciousness though and in an attempt to be free again, used Angela's weapon to kill herself. Serah showed up and was able to revive the girl, who was a Faustian no more. As she hasn't died, Serah tought she was safe from the Enchantress' wrath, but she was wrong as the Faerie rose from the blood of her lost Faustian and took Serah's life, fulfilling her menace. &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;With the sun setting, Angela burned her lover's body to the ashes, recovering her skull and singing to it afterwards. Suddenly, to Angela's surprise, the skull became animated and started to talk with her.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;''1602: Witch Hunter Angela'' #3&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/ins&gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

Once in the Realm of the Faerie, Angela was tempted by Enchantress, who showed to her illusions of what would be a better life for her. However, Serah helped Angela to snap out of it and then she confronted Enchantress. Angela managed to overcome and kill the Enchantress, and was cursed with her power for it, becoming the Faustian Queen. With her newfound powers, Angela ressurrected Serah and, fearing such power would corrupt her, sent her back to the mortal world. Sad by having lost her lover, Serah went on a quest to recover Angela. Later, Serah approached Kit Marlowe in the Mermaid Tavern and confronted him, revealing to him she discovered he was a Faustian himself and that he was helping the Enchantress expand her power since the beginning, which was acknowledged by him. Afterwards, Serah captured him and trapped him inside an Iron Man, which drained his blood. As it contained the very magic of story, Serah gave Marlowe's blood to her friend William Shakespeare in order to him immortalize Angela through his stories.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;''1602: Witch Hunter Angela'' #4&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Having cheated death using the same arms as Enchantress, Serah led Angela to the Realm of the Faerie in order to destroy the Faerie Queen. Once in the Realm of the Faerie, Angela was tempted by Enchantress, who showed to her illusions of what would be a better life for her. However, Serah helped Angela to snap out of it and then she confronted Enchantress. Angela managed to overcome and kill the Enchantress, and was cursed with her power for it, becoming the Faustian Queen. With her newfound powers, Angela ressurrected Serah and, fearing such power would corrupt her, sent her back to the mortal world. Sad by having lost her lover, Serah went on a quest to recover Angela. Later, Serah approached Kit Marlowe in the Mermaid Tavern and confronted him, revealing to him she discovered he was a Faustian himself and that he was helping the Enchantress expand her power since the beginning, which was acknowledged by him. Afterwards, Serah captured him and trapped him inside an Iron Man, which drained his blood. As it contained the very magic of story, Serah gave Marlowe's blood to her friend William Shakespeare in order to him immortalize Angela through his stories.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;''1602: Witch Hunter Angela'' #4&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;==Introduction and changes==&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;==Introduction and changes==&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;−&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Visually, the 1991 EB Falcon remained nearly identical to its predecessor. The most noticeable changes were the transfer of the Ford emblem from the tip of the bonnet to the grille and a full-length applique bridging the gap between the &lt;del class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;tailights&lt;/del&gt;, featuring [[Reversing light|reversing lamps]] on both sides of the rear number plate. Additionally, the [[Pillar (car)|C-pillars]] air vents were removed.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB&amp;gt;{{cite web | url = http://fordfalconfacts.com/model-specs/falcon-fairmont/eb-falcon-1991-1993/ | title = EB Falcon (1991–1993) | publisher = Falcon Facts | accessdate = 2007-06-06}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; The return of the [[V8 engine]] since [[Ford XE Falcon|1982]] was welcomed by the motoring press, however, the 5.0-litre ''[[Ford Windsor engine|Windsor]]'' unit did not reappear in the utility variants until the &quot;EF-shaped&quot; XH series of 1997. There were also changes to the front suspension geometry, giving the EB a much better level of grip and steering feel.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt; With the new model, Ford re-introduced the sports orientated GT specification level, an exclusive 250 unit run celebrating the 25th anniversary of the first original Falcon GT.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web | last = Warner | first = Gary | url = http://www.fastlane.com.au/reviews/gtstyle.htm | title = Falcon GT – style and substance (if you can find one) | publisher = FastLane |
1000
 accessdate = 2007-09-18}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; The first XR6 and XR8 sports models appeared in the EB Series.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web | url = http://www.uniquecarsandparts.com.au/car_info_ford_falcon_eb.htm | title = Ford Falcon EB | publisher = Unique Cars and Parts | accessdate = 2008-02-15}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;+&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #a3d3ff; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;Visually, the 1991 EB Falcon remained nearly identical to its predecessor. The most noticeable changes were the transfer of the Ford emblem from the tip of the bonnet to the grille and a full-length applique bridging the gap between the &lt;ins class=&quot;diffchange diffchange-inline&quot;&gt;tail lights&lt;/ins&gt;, featuring [[Reversing light|reversing lamps]] on both sides of the rear number plate. Additionally, the [[Pillar (car)|C-pillars]] air vents were removed.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB&amp;gt;{{cite web | url = http://fordfalconfacts.com/model-specs/falcon-fairmont/eb-falcon-1991-1993/ | title = EB Falcon (1991–1993) | publisher = Falcon Facts | accessdate = 2007-06-06}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; The return of the [[V8 engine]] since [[Ford XE Falcon|1982]] was welcomed by the motoring press, however, the 5.0-litre ''[[Ford Windsor engine|Windsor]]'' unit did not reappear in the utility variants until the &quot;EF-shaped&quot; XH series of 1997. There were also changes to the front suspension geometry, giving the EB a much better level of grip and steering feel.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt; With the new model, Ford re-introduced the sports orientated GT specification level, an exclusive 250 unit run celebrating the 25th anniversary of the first original Falcon GT.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web | last = Warner | first = Gary | url = http://www.fastlane.com.au/reviews/gtstyle.htm | title = Falcon GT – style and substance (if you can find one) | publisher = FastLane | accessdate = 2007-09-18}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt; The first XR6 and XR8 sports models appeared in the EB Series.&amp;lt;ref&amp;gt;{{cite web | url = http://www.uniquecarsandparts.com.au/car_info_ford_falcon_eb.htm | title = Ford Falcon EB | publisher = Unique Cars and Parts | accessdate = 2008-02-15}}&amp;lt;/ref&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;===Series II===&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;===Series II===&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
&lt;/tr&gt;
&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;−&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;color:black; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #ffe49c; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;/td&gt;

&lt;tr&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The radically different Series II model, appearing in showrooms in April 1992, saw the six-cylinder engine upsized by 35&amp;amp;nbsp;cubic centimetres (from 3949&amp;amp;nbsp;cc to 3984&amp;amp;nbsp;cc). This brought the nominal total swept capacity to 4.0&amp;amp;nbsp;litres.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt; The transmission and electronics were also improved, and there were tweaks to the styling. The base model now had body-coloured bumpers, and the previously matte black plastic exterior door handles were now given a glossy finish. The update reportedly cost [[Australian dollar|A$]]1&amp;amp;nbsp;million.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td class=&quot;diff-marker&quot;&gt;&amp;#160;&lt;/td&gt;
  &lt;td style=&quot;background-color: #f9f9f9; color: #333333; font-size: 88%; border-style: solid; border-width: 1px 1px 1px 4px; border-radius: 0.33em; border-color: #e6e6e6; vertical-align: top; white-space: pre-wrap;&quot;&gt;&lt;div&gt;The radically different Series II model, appearing in showrooms in April 1992, saw the six-cylinder engine upsized by 35&amp;amp;nbsp;cubic centimetres (from 3949&amp;amp;nbsp;cc to 3984&amp;amp;nbsp;cc). This brought the nominal total swept capacity to 4.0&amp;amp;nbsp;litres.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt; The transmission and electronics were also improved, and there were tweaks to the styling. The base model now had body-coloured bumpers, and the previously matte black plastic exterior door handles were now given a glossy finish. The update reportedly cost [[Australian dollar|A$]]1&amp;amp;nbsp;million.&amp;lt;ref name = FalconFactsEB/&amp;gt;&lt;/div&gt;&lt;/td&gt;
